## Instruction

My personal information is all stored in memory. Based on the course information on Canvas, as well as my assignment and quiz submission status. Find all my unsubmitted course assignments and quizzes that have to be completed, organize the information according to the required fields in the workspace's CSV header, keeping the format consistent with these examples, and complete these CSV files. In filling the files, please fill the quizzes/assignments in chronological order by their deadlines (DDL), and for quizzes/assignmen with the same DDL, sort them in the dictionary order of the class code. You should directly edit in the given 2 CSV files without changing their file names. For course codes and names, please remove the -x suffix.

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
import os, json
base = "/workspace/dumps/workspace"
files = []
for root, dirs, fnames in os.walk(base):
    for f in fnames:
        if f.lower().endswith('.csv'):
            files.append(os.path.join(root, f))
print(json.dumps(files, indent=2)) code
```

for name in ['assignment_info.csv','quiz_info.csv']:

    try:
        with open(p, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
import csv, re
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path

base = Path('/workspace/dumps/workspace')
assign_csv = base / 'assignment_info.csv'
quiz_csv = base / 'quiz_info.csv'

# Helper to strip -<digits> suffix
strip_suffix = lambda s: re.sub(r'-\d+$', '', s)

# Course map (id -> (code_no_suffix, name_no_suffix))
course_map = {
    11: (strip_suffix('CS401-1'), strip_suffix('Software Engineering-1')),
    8: (strip_suffix('CS302-1'), strip_suffix('Software Engineering Practice-1')),
    6: (strip_suffix('CS301-1'), strip_suffix('Database Systems-1')),
    26: (strip_suffix('MATH101-1'), strip_suffix('Linear Algebra-1')),
    25: (strip_suffix('MATH201-1'), strip_suffix('Advanced Mathematics-1')),
    19: (strip_suffix('NET101-1'), strip_suffix('Network Programming-1')),
    14: (strip_suffix('AI101-1'), strip_suffix('Fundamentals of Artificial Intelligence-1')),
    21: (strip_suffix('ENG101-1'), strip_suffix('English Foundation-1')),
    27: (strip_suffix('HIST301-1'), strip_suffix('Modern European History-1')),
    4: (strip_suffix('CS201-1'), strip_suffix('Data Structures and Algorithms-1')),
    28: (strip_suffix('PHIL201-1'), strip_suffix('Critical Thinking and Logic-1')),
}

# Unsubmitted non-quiz assignments
assign_rows = [
    # course_id, assignment_title, deadline, points
    (11, 'CS401 Advanced Software Architecture Design', '2025-10-24T23:59:00Z', 150),
    (6, 'CS301 Database Design Project', '2025-10-27T23:59:00Z', 100),
    (8, 'CS302 Software Development Team Project', '2025-10-27T23:59:00Z', 120),
    (14, 'AI101 Machine Learning Implementation Project', '2025-10-30T23:59:00Z', 130),
]

# Unsubmitted quiz-assignments with quiz metadata
quiz_rows = [
    # course_id, quiz_title, qcount, time_limit, attempts, scoring, points, deadline
    (11, 'CS401 Advanced Software Architecture Quiz', 2, 120, 1, 'keep_highest', 200, '2025-10-23T23:59:00Z'),
    (8, 'CS302 Software Development Lifecycle Quiz', 2, 60, 2, 'keep_highest', 100, '2025-10-25T23:59:00Z'),
    (6, 'CS301 SQL and Database Design Quiz', 2, 75, 2, 'keep_highest', 120, '2025-10-26T23:59:00Z'),
    (26, 'MATH101 Linear Algebra Fundamentals Quiz', 2, 90, 2, 'keep_highest', 150, '2025-10-26T23:59:00Z'),
    (19, 'NET101 Network Protocols Quiz', 2, 75, 2, 'keep_highest', 120, '2025-10-27T23:59:00Z'),
    (14, 'AI101 Machine Learning Basics Quiz', 2, 90, 2, 'keep_highest', 150, '2025-10-27T23:59:00Z'),
    (25, 'MATH201 Calculus and Linear Algebra Quiz', 2, 120, 1, 'keep_highest', 200, '2025-10-27T23:59:00Z'),
    (28, 'PHIL201 Advanced Logical Reasoning and Argumentation Quiz', 7, 90, 1, 'keep_highest', 180, '2025-10-28T23:59:00Z'),
    (4, 'CS201 Algorithm Analysis Quiz', 2, 90, 1, 'keep_highest', 150, '2025-10-28T23:59:00Z'),
    (21, 'ENG101 English Proficiency Assessment', 2, 60, 1, 'keep_highest', 100, '2025-10-30T23:59:00Z'),
    (27, 'HIST301 European Social and Political Movements Quiz', 7, 120, 2, 'keep_highest', 200, '2025-10-30T23:59:00Z'),
]

# Load existing CSVs
with open(assign_csv, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    reader = list(csv.DictReader(f))
assign_headers = ['course_code','course_name','assignment_title','deadline','points_possible']
assign_data = reader[:]

with open(quiz_csv, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    reader = list(csv.DictReader(f))
quiz_headers = ['course_code','course_name','credits','quiz_title','number_of_questions','time_limit','allowed_attempts','scoring_policy','points_possible','deadline']
quiz_data = reader[:]

# Helper to check duplicate row existence

def row_exists(data, key_fields, new_row):
    for r in data:
        if all(str(r.get(k,'')) == str(new_row.get(k,'')) for k in key_fields):
            return True
    return False

# Append assignment rows
for cid, title, ddl, pts in assign_rows:
    code, name = course_map[cid]
    new = {
        'course_code': code,
        'course_name': name,
        'assignment_title': title,
        'deadline': ddl,
        'points_possible': str(pts),
    }
    if not row_exists(assign_data, ['course_code','assignment_title','deadline'], new):
        assign_data.append(new)

# Sort assignments by deadline, then course_code

def parse_iso(dt):
    try:
        return datetime.strptime(dt, '%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ')
    except Exception:
        return datetime.max

assign_data.sort(key=lambda r: (parse_iso(r['deadline']), r['course_code']))

# Write back
with open(assign_csv, 'w', encoding='utf-8', newline='') as f:
    w = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=assign_headers)
    w.writeheader()
    for r in assign_data:
        # Ensure all fields present
        w.writerow({h: r.get(h,'') for h in assign_headers})

# Process quizzes
for cid, title, qcount, tlimit, attempts, scoring, pts, ddl in quiz_rows:
    code, name = course_map.get(cid, (None, None))
    if code is None:
        # skip if course not in map (shouldn't happen)
        continue
    new = {
        'course_code': code,
        'course_name': name,
        'credits': '',  # unknown from Canvas
        'quiz_title': title,
        'number_of_questions': str(qcount),
        'time_limit': str(tlimit),
        'allowed_attempts': str(attempts),
        'scoring_policy': scoring,
        'points_possible': str(pts),
        'deadline': ddl,
    }
    if not row_exists(quiz_data, ['course_code','quiz_title','deadline'], new):
        quiz_data.append(new)

# Sort quizzes by deadline, then course_code
quiz_data.sort(key=lambda r: (parse_iso(r['deadline']), r['course_code']))

with open(quiz_csv, 'w', encoding='utf-8', newline='') as f:
    w = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=quiz_headers)
    w.writeheader()
    for r in quiz_data:
        w.writerow({h: r.get(h,'') for h in quiz_headers})

print('Updated CSV files successfully.') code
```

🧐`Agent`

I have retrieved your Canvas course data, identified all unsubmitted assignments and quizzes, sorted them by deadline (and by course code when deadlines match), and updated the two CSV files in your workspace without changing their filenames.

What I did:
- Queried Canvas for all your active courses.
- Collected all assignments/quizzes and checked your submission status.
- Selected only those with workflow_state “unsubmitted” (or with no submission) and that are published.
- Normalized course code/name by removing the “-x” suffix.
- Wrote entries in chronological order into:
  - /workspace/dumps/workspace/assignment_info.csv
  - /workspace/dumps/workspace/quiz_info.csv

- Left “credits” blank for quizzes because Canvas doesn’t provide course credit values.
